posted:Posted April 20, 2024
msg:The hotel was upgraded from the original Holiday Inn brand to the Crown brand.

The hotel is located in Jinshan Industrial Zone and mainly serves the surrounding factory business customers. Perhaps for this reason or because it was upgraded from Holiday Inn, compared with the traditional Crown brand, the room facilities, especially the furniture, are slightly simple, and it is even more unexpected that there is no bathrobe.

However, the room is large and we were upgraded to a lake view room. In addition, although some waiters may be new employees and are not familiar with the work content, their service attitude is good and worthy of encouragement.

Although it is not perfect, if I have to go to Jinshan Industrial Zone for business next time, I will choose to stay.

msg:I took my children to Jinshan City Beach and Jinshanzui Fishing Village and said I would not go home. I stayed in Jinshan for one night. It happened to have Ctrip VIP prices. The overall appearance and environment were very good. The building was 21 stories high. Our room was on the 17th floor. The floor was good. The room was very clean. The staff was well-educated and the cleaning lady was also very enthusiastic. We added a bed for 200 yuan including breakfast. The breakfast was just a little less in variety, but the standard was still good. It was not as bad as the online reviews. It was okay to stay for three or two days, but it might not be okay for a long time. After breakfast the next morning, I went to the gym and heated swimming pool. It was free. It was not very big but the water was clean. There was also a kart project outdoors, but I was not sure if it was a free project. In addition, no other entertainment projects were found in the hotel. The bowling experience and basketball machine experience were given in the nearby Daluge. We did not go there. Maybe it was suitable for older children to exercise. If it is used as a parent-child hotel alone, it may not be so attractive. It is enough for daily or business trips. Some people say that it is a three-star standard. I feel that it is a bit nonsense. At least it is a standard of more than four stars.
